<div id="review_1724716459" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1724716459" />
    <a title="Sandy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/24770184-sandy"><img alt="Sandy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1385133529p2/24770184.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1724716459?book_show_action=true">Aug 10, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sandy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sandy" href="/user/show/24770184-sandy">Sandy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24770184-sandy?shelf=contemporary-fiction">contemporary-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24770184-sandy?shelf=black-humour">black-humour</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24770184-sandy?shelf=political-intrigue">political-intrigue</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24770184-sandy?shelf=arc-from-netgalley">arc-from-netgalley</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24770184-sandy?shelf=conspiracies">conspiracies</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24770184-sandy?shelf=crime">crime</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24770184-sandy?shelf=family-drama">family-drama</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24770184-sandy?shelf=suspense">suspense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24770184-sandy?shelf=private-eye">private-eye</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24770184-sandy?shelf=legal-thriller">legal-thriller</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1724716459" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15832561421990923947">Canon 7 of the ABA moral code of responsibility states “a lawyer should represent his client zealously within the bounds of the law”. Attorney Peter Donley takes it to heart but puts his own spin on just how far he should go to save his client.<br/><br/>Father Tom Martin runs a shelter for troubled boys. When one is found murdered, the DA wastes no time naming him as the killer. Peter works with his Uncle Lou who has made a career out of defending the disadvantaged. But when Lou ends up in hospital, the c</span>
  <span id="freeText15832561421990923947" style="display:none">Canon 7 of the ABA moral code of responsibility states “a lawyer should represent his client zealously within the bounds of the law”. Attorney Peter Donley takes it to heart but puts his own spin on just how far he should go to save his client.<br /><br />Father Tom Martin runs a shelter for troubled boys. When one is found murdered, the DA wastes no time naming him as the killer. Peter works with his Uncle Lou who has made a career out of defending the disadvantaged. But when Lou ends up in hospital, the case falls to Peter &amp; he’s quickly swept up in a conspiracy of lies, revenge &amp; family secrets.<br />There’s something fishy about the case &amp; Peter hires PI Frank Ross to help with the investigation. Ross used to be a cop &amp; knows all the players well. But there’s another layer to the story involving powerful men who will do anything to keep the truth buried &amp; Peter is soon way out of his comfort zone.<br /><br />The story is set in 1987 but was written in 1996. I enjoyed this author’s Tracy Crosswhite series &amp; it’s interesting to note the evolution of his style. Initially I found some of the other characters more compelling than Peter but as the story progressed &amp; he began to colour outside the lines a bit, I became a fan.<br /><br />The addition of Frank Ross is a turning point &amp; it’s the relationship between these 2 men that spurs the plot forward. On the outside, they couldn’t be more different. But they share a similar code of ethics &amp; desire to uncover the truth that puts them in synch &amp; I enjoyed their interaction. Each has a rich back story that is slowly revealed &amp; informs their motivations. Strong secondary characters, believable dialogue &amp; atmospheric settings add to the story. <br /><br />It’s a smart, fast paced legal thriller that begs the question……soooo…..Mr. Dugoni, there are 8 more canons in the ABA’s code. When can we expect the next one?<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="15832561421990923947" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('smCwE/E4+LQhbt16Gvf2MZ1PRZwkDtIYwpWvD/j6XxiIRtnBSmYx3IZFaRvtAvzuSxCiVOqDXH+Z6+m+Nbmtgg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('IuVEUScwAWfG56qFjP+4XTjE5xZe+bUJVVE/3JgUBPcYwy2DnG7ID2HMHuR7CrKC7psA3pB0O24OL3ltVVf2bQ==')})
  }

          <div class='bookAuthorProfile'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__topContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__photoContainer'>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer330840566923366586">Robert Dugoni is the New York Times, #1 Amazon, and #1 Wall Street Journal Bestselling Author of the Tracy Crosswhite series: My Sister's Grave, Her Last Breath, In the Clearing, The Trapped Girl and Close to Home, A Steep Price and A Cold Trail as well as the short prequels The Academy and Third Watch. The police procedural featuring Seattle Homicide Detective Tracy Crosswhite has kept Dugoni in </span>
  <span id="freeText330840566923366586" style="display:none">Robert Dugoni is the New York Times, #1 Amazon, and #1 Wall Street Journal Bestselling Author of the Tracy Crosswhite series: My Sister's Grave, Her Last Breath, In the Clearing, The Trapped Girl and Close to Home, A Steep Price and A Cold Trail as well as the short prequels The Academy and Third Watch. The police procedural featuring Seattle Homicide Detective Tracy Crosswhite has kept Dugoni in the Amazon top 10 for more than three years and sold more than 5 million copies. He is also the author of the critically acclaimed The Extraordinary Life of Sam Hell, released April 2018 and soon to be a major motion picture. He is also the author of the Charles Jenkin's International spy series, The Eighth Sister and The Last Agent, soon to be a television series. Dugoni's first series featured attorney David Sloane and CIA agent Charles Jenkins. <br />He is the winner of the Nancy Pearl Award for fiction, a two-time nominee for the Harper Lee Award for Legal Fiction, A two-time nominee for the Mystery Writer's of America Edgar Award and a two-time nominee for the International Thriller of the year. His non-fiction expose, The Cyanide Canary, was a 2004 Best Book of the Year. He is published in more than 30 countries and two dozen languages.<br />You can sign up for his newsletter at:<br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.robertdugoni.com">http://www.robertdugoni.com</a> and message him on facebook, twitter and instagram </span>
  <a data-text-id="330840566923366586" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      <div class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/work/quotes/50278266-the-7th-canon">Quotes from The 7th Canon</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class="stacked" tyle="padding-bottom:15px">
            <span class="readable">&ldquo;The past is always the highest peak, and the hardest to scale. But when you finally pull yourself to the top and peer over the edge, there’s nothing before you but the rest of your life.&rdquo;</span>
            <nobr>
              &mdash;
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/quotes/8525607-the-past-is-always-the-highest-peak-and-the-hardest">2 likes</a>
            </nobr>
            <div class="clear"></div>
          </div>
          <div class="stacked" tyle="padding-bottom:15px">
            <span class="readable">&ldquo;People say the justice system is color-blind, but it isn’t. It sees color, and it sees green. It will always see green. We like to think our courts are the great equalizer between the powerful and the powerless, but more times than not, money and power still prevail. To the Jack Devines of this world, Bennet wasn’t the victim because in Jack Devine’s way of thinking, everything was OK because he paid for it.&rdquo;</span>
            <nobr>
              &mdash;
